[\[10b.1\]]nas tsam gyis tshod par bri'o/_/shar phyogs su ni dkar po che/_/lho phyogs ser po dang ldan pa/_/nub kyi cha ni dmar po'o/_/byang phyogs ljang dang ldan pa'o/_/in+d+ra nI la'i 'od ldan pa/_/dbus kyi cha ni mnyam par bri/_/de ltar dkyil 'khor bris nas su/_/lha'i gnas

[\[14a.1\]]gding ngo /_/de'i tshad sum 'gyur gyi skud pas bcings te/_las thams cad pa'i sngags bzlas pas bsrung ngo /_/de nas/_thams cad mkhyen nyid 'jig rten du/_/brgya la 'byung ngam mi 'byung 'gyur/_/u dum bA ra'i me tog kyang /_/res 'ga' res 'ga' 'byung ba

[\[14b.1\]]do/_/zhes brjod nas/_bdag dang slob ma 'jug pa'i cho ga yin te/_dang po slob dpon dkyil 'khor du zhugs shing dbang thams cad rdzogs par bya ste/_rjes su gnang ba thob nas/_yol ba'i phyi rol du yon phul ba'i slob ma dbang bskur ba'i snod du gyur pa/_rnam par snang
[\[14b.2\]]mdzad kyi gzugs su dmigs la/_A khaM bI ra hUM zhes bya ba'i sngags bzla zhing me tog gi phreng ba bzung ste/_mig gnyis bkab pa las thams cad pa'i sngags kyis btab pa'i chus bsangs te/_dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa'i phyir/_/khyod gang la dga' ba yin zhes dri'o/_/des kyang
[\[14b.3\]]skal bzang bdag ni bde ba chen po la'o zhes brjod do/_/de ma thag tu oM sarba yo ga tsit+ta ut+pA da yA mi zhes bya bas rnal 'byor gyi sems bskyed par bya'o/_/de nas me tog gi phreng ba dang bcas pa'i rdo rje snying gar bzhag la/_oM su ra te sa ma ya s+t+waM ho tiSh+Tha badzra ya thA su khaM zhes bya'o/_/_
[\[14b.4\]]de nas sngar bstan pa'i yi ge lnga brjod cing /_yol ba'i nang du bkug la 'di skad ces brjod do/_/de ring khyed sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs su zhugs kyis de bas na ye shes rdo rje de ngas bskyed par bya'o/_/ye shes gang gis de kho na nyid kyi dngos grub kyang 'thob na/_dngos grub
[\[14b.5\]]gzhan lta smos kyang ci dgos/_khyed kyis dkyil 'khor ma mthong ba rnams kyi mdun du brjod par mi bya ste/_dam tshig nyams par gyur ta re/_de nas de'i spyi bor rdo rje bzhag la 'di skad ces brjod do/_/'di ni dam tshig rdo rje ste/_/gal te khyod kyis 'di 'ga' la/_/smras na mgo bo 'gas
[\[14b.6\]]par 'gyur/_/rdo rje sems dpa' rang nyid ni/_/de ring khyod kyi snying la gnas/_/gal te tshul 'di smras na ni/_/de yi mod la bkas nas gshegs/_/zhes bya ba 'dis mna' bsgag go/_/tsan+dan dang gur kum bsres pa'i chu la oM badzra u da ka ThaHzhes lan bdun gyi bar du bzlas la/_
[\[14b.7\]]'di ni dmyal ba'i chu yin te/_/dam tshig nyams na sreg par byed/_/dam tshig bsrungs na 'grub 'gyur ba'i/_/rdo rje bdud rtsi'i chu 'thung shig/_/ces brjod la blud do/_/de nas 'di skad brjod de/_de ring phan chad khyod kyi phyag na rdo rje nga yin gyis/_ngas gang smras pa de khyod kyis bya ba yin no/_/_
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]nga la brnyas par ma byed cig_/nyam nga ba ma spangs par 'chi ba'i dus byas nas/_dmyal bar ltung bar ma byed cig ces brjod do/_/de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin brlabs nas/_rdo rje sems dpa' bdag la dbab tu gsol/_/zhes brjod do/_/_
[\[15a.2\]]de'i spyi bor yi ge baM las byung ba'i bum pas mtshan ma dkar po chu'i dkyil 'khor zlum po dkyil du ha'o/_/snying gar laM las byung ba'i dbang chen gyi dkyil 'khor ser po gru bzhi/_rdo rje rtse gsum pas mtshams su mtshan pa de la hUM ngo /_/lte bar raM las byung ba'i me'i dkyil 'khor
[\[15a.3\]]gru gsum pa dmar po shin tu rno zhing tsha ba de la A'o/_/rkang pa'i 'og tu yaM las byung ba rlung gi dkyil 'khor sngon po gzhu'i rnam pa lta bu g.yo ba'i ba dan phyed pas mtshan pa de la dz+haiHdrag cing rno ba 'bar ba'i phung po de rlung gi bum par bsams la ji srid me'i dkyil 'khor gzhan
[\[15a.4\]]gyi bar du'o/_/de dag g.yos par gyur nas 'bar zhing byung bas dbang chen gyi dkyil 'khor yang 'bar bar gyur to/_/de nas chu'i dkyil 'khor las dag cing gtsang ba'i rgyun bab pas/_/ngoms shing tshim par gyur nas rlung gis bteg pa dang /_slob ma dang rang 'gying bag dang
[\[15a.5\]]bcas pa'i khro bo chen po gshin rje mthar byed sku shin tu drag po can/_phyag g.yas pas rdo rje gsor ba/_g.yon pas dril bu 'khrol ba 'bebs pa'i sngags kyis phab ste/_spos dbul lo/_/de'i sngags ni 'di yin te/_oM hrIHSh+T-iHwi kr-i tA na na hUM phaT phaT A be sha ya s+t+waM b+ha ya ra ra
[\[15a.6\]]ra ra tsA le hUM ha A dz+haiHphaT ces bya bas myur du phebs par 'gyur ro/_/de nas 'dod chags gshin rje gshed du de ma thag tu dmigs la/_de'i lce la yi ge AHdmar po bsams te/_tiSh+Tha badzra zhes brjod do/_/rdo rje chos ni mgon po che/_/'od dpag med ni bde ba che/_/smros shig 'dod
[\[15a.7\]]chags chos chen po/_/dge dang mi dge ba de 'dri/_/babs na dge dang mi dge de/_/ngag gi brtan pa rjod par byed/_/sems ni brtan nas khams gsum dag/_/shes shing lus ni brtan gyur na/_/nam mkha' la yang 'gro bar 'gyur/_/gal te ring du 'gro 'gyur na/_/mgo bo'i gtsug tu laM
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]las byung ba'i dbang chen gyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs rdo rjes kun nas mnan par bsgoms la de rengs par bya'o/_/de lta bu ni dbab pa'o/_/de nas thogs pa'i me tog de dkyil 'khor du dbul zhing pra tIts+tsha badzra ho zhes brjod do/_/de ltar lha gang gi gnas mtshan ma dang nye bar bab par gyur na de'i
[\[15b.2\]]rigs yin par de la bstan par bya'o/_/gnas mchog tu bab na dngos grub mchog 'grub bo/_/gnas dkyil du ni dngos grub 'bring ngo /_/gnas smad kyi las dngos grub tha ma'o/_/dkyil 'khor gyi phyi rol tu bab na dngos grub med do/_/gal te dkyil 'khor du ma bab na de yang 'phang
[\[15b.3\]]ngo /_/lan gsum 'phangs kyang de nyid du ma bab na de gzung bar mi bya'o/_/de ni me tog dor ba'o/_/phangs pa'i phreng ba de blangs te de'i mgo la bcings la/_sems can stobs po che 'di longs shig ces brjod do/_/de nas/_oM rdo rje sems dpa' rang nyid ni/_/de ring khyed kyi mig 'byed
[\[15b.4\]]mdzad/_/de ltar mig ni thams cad 'byed/_/rdo rje mig ni bla med pa/_/zhes brjod nas gdong g.yogs dbye'o/_/de nas dkyil 'khor gyi lha so so'i ming bstan pa sngon du 'gro bas/_byang phyogs kyi sgo nas brtsams te/_gtso bo'i bar du bstan par bya'o/_/de ni dkyil 'khor du 'jug
[\[15b.5\]]pa'o/_/de nas sangs rgyas chos chen po/_/rdo rje sems dpas dbang bskur ltar/_/bdag kyang mgon pos dbang bskur zhing /_/nyid kyi mchog kyang stsal du gsol/_/zhes bya bas gsol ba 'debs pa dang ldan pa'i slob ma bzung la/_rdo rje tsartsi ka la sogs pas bum pas dbang bskur ro/_/_
[\[15b.6\]]rdo rje chen pos dbang bskur ba/_/khams gsum po yi phyag byas pa/_/gsang gsum pa yi gnas byung ba'i/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis sbyin par bya/_/zhes brjod cing las thams cad pa bzlas pa'i bum pa'i chu rdo rje khu tshur gyis kun nas gtor zhing /_oM badzra a b+hi Shiny+tsa zhes brjod do/_slob ma
[\[15b.7\]]'khor los sgyur ba bzhin du dbang bskur ro/_/chu'i dbang bskur ba'o/_/de nas gser ram gos las bsgrubs pa'i cod pan ji lta ba'i sngags kyis mgo'i steng du bzhag la nam mkha'i khongs su gtogs pa'i rang gi rigs kyi gzugs su cod pan la bzhugs su gsol te sbyin pa ni cod pan gyi
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]dbang bskur ba'o/_/de'i rjes la rdo rje byin la/_sangs rgyas rdo rje dbang bskur bas/_/de ring khyod ni dbang bskur bya/_/'di de sangs rgyas thams cad nyid/_/rdo rje long shig rab 'grub 'gyur/_/zhes brjod cing rdo rje snying ga la sogs par reg la lag pa g.yas par
[\[16a.2\]]sbyin pa ni rdo rje'i dbang bskur ba'o/_/de nas lag pa g.yon par dril bu byin la/_rdo rje dril bu dang ldan pa'i lag pa dag gis 'khyud pa ltar byas te/_oM badzra a d+hi pa ti s+t+waM a b+hi Shiny+tsA mi tiSh+Tha badzra sa ma ya s+t+waM zhes brjod la sbyin te/_de ni dril bu'i dbang bskur ba'o/_/de nyid la
[\[16a.3\]]bdag po'i dbang zhes kyang bya'o/_/de nas rdo rje dril bu spyi bor bzung la/_oM badzra satwa s+t+waM a b+hi Shiny+tsA mi badzra nA ma a b+hi She ka ta/_kye dpal che ge mo rdo rje zhes bya ba la sogs pas/_rigs dang rjes su mthun pa'i ming gdags so/_/dbang 'di dag gis sngags dang rgyud bshad pa dang /_gsang
[\[16a.4\]]sngags sgrub pa la dbang bar 'gyur ro/_/'di ni dbang lnga pa ste/_rtsa ba'i yin no/_/rtsa ba'i dbang thams cad la yang tsartsi ka la sogs pa'i bya ba thams cad yin pa nyid do/_/de nas rtsa ba'i dbang mnos pas slob dpon sdom pa can/_kye snying rje'i gter bdag dang gzhan gyi don
[\[16a.5\]]nus pa'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang de khyed kyi sku drin gyis stsal du gsol zhes gsol ba gdab pa dang ldan pas dkyil 'khor dang nye bar rdul tshon dmar po las byas pa'i pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad pa'i steng du gor stan la bzhag ste/_rdo rje tsartsi ka la sogs pas dbang bskur zhing dam
[\[16a.6\]]tshig gsum bzung ngo /_/de la dam tshig gsum ni 'di yin te/_hUM las rdo rje bsgoms la/_khams gsum pa yi ral gri che/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis phyag byas pa/_/'di ni las kyi ral gri mchog/_/dgra rnams las rgyal bya phyir zung /_/zhes bya bas de kho na nyid kyi rdo rje gzung
[\[16a.7\]]ngo /_/'di ni rdo rje'i dam tshig go/_/de nas AHlas byung ba'i dril bu la shes rab dang /_thabs kyi ngo bo nyid rdo rje dang dril bu 'dis 'grub par 'gyur gyis zung shig_/bu rdo rje khyod kyis slob ma la yang zung shig ces byas la/_de'i lag par byin te/_srid pa ngo bo nyid kyis dag_/ngo bo
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]nyid kyis dngos med byas/_/sems can rang bzhin rtag tu dag_/srid pa'i mchog ni byed pa yin/_/zhes bya bas de la gdams par bya ste/_'di ni dril bu'i dam tshig go/_/de nas phyag rgya'i dam tshig bstan te/_yid kyi gzugs ni brtan pa nyid/_/phyag rgya yin par
[\[16b.2\]]rab grags te/_/'di yis rang gi 'dod lha ni/_/bdag nyid phyag rgya chen por gnas/_/zhes bya ba ni phyag rgya'i dam tshig go/_/de nas dkyil 'khor gyi de kho na nyid dang lha'i de kho na nyid dang slob dpon gyi las dang dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa dang /_slob dpon 'jug pa'i bya ba bstan
[\[16b.3\]]par bya'o/_/de la sangs rgyas dang /_sangs rgyas ma yin pa bdag de kho na nyid du mnyam pas gru bzhi pa'o/_/lus dang /_tshor ba dang sems dang /_chos rnams gcig dang du ma dang bral bas gzugs brnyan dang mtshungs pa nyid la/_dad pa rnam par dag pa ni shar phyogs kyi sgo'o/_/_
[\[16b.4\]]skyes pa dang ma skyes pa'i mi dge ba'i chos spang ba dang /_mi bskyed pa dang /_skyes pa dang ma skyes pa'i dge ba'i chos 'phel zhing rgyas par bya ba dang /_bskyed pa'i phyir rtsom pa'i las dang /_rtog pa'i bdag nyid kyis brtson 'grus bzhi po rnam par dag pa ni lho'i sgo'o/_/'dun pa dang brtson
[\[16b.5\]]'grus dang /_sems dang /_dpyod pa zhes bya ba rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang /_gang dran pa rnam par dag pa ni nub kyi sgo'o/_/dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang /_dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang /_shes rab ces bya ba dbang po lnga'i ting nge 'dzin rnam par dag pa ni byang gi sgo'o/_/rtog pa dang /_dpyod pa
[\[16b.6\]]dang /_dga' ba dang /_bde ba dang sems rtse gcig pa zhes bya ba bsam gtan dang po'i yan lag dang /_rtog pa dang dpyod pa spangs pa bsam gtan gnyis pa dang /_dga' ba yang spangs shing btang snyoms dang /_dran pa dang ldan pas bsam gtan gsum pa dang /_btang snyoms dang
[\[16b.7\]]dran pa dag pa dang /_sdug bsngal yang ma yin/_bde ba yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba bsam gtan bzhi pa rnam par dag pa ni/_rta babs bzhi'o/_/dpa' bar 'gro ba dang /_nam mkha' mdzod dang /_dri ma med pa dang /_seng ge rnam par rol pa'i ting nge 'dzin bzhi po rnam par dag pa ni kha
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]khyer bzhi'o/_/don dang tshig dang /_nges tshig dang /_spobs pa bzhi dang /_gzungs bzhi rnam par dag pa ni kha khyer la gnas pa'i mchod pa'i lha mo'i tshogs so/_/bsam pa thams cad rdzogs pas ni rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs so/_/mdo dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa
[\[17a.2\]]dang /_lung du bstan pa dang /_tshigs su bcad pa dang /_ched du brjod pa dang /_gleng gzhi dang /_skyes pa'i rabs dang /_shin tu rgyas pa dang /_rmad du byung ba gsung rab yan lag dgu gdul bya'i skye bo la bstan pa rnam par dag pa ni/_dril bu dang g.yer kha'i sgra dang ba dan no/_/dran pa
[\[17a.3\]]dang chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa dang /_brtson 'grus dang dga' ba dang shin tu sbyangs pa dang /_ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms zhes bya ba byang chub kyi yan lag bdun rnam par dag pa ni/_dra ba dang dra ba phyed pa dang /_me long dang me tog gi phreng ba dang /_rnga yab 'bar ba'o/_/nang gzugs med
[\[17a.4\]]pa'i 'du shes kyis phyi rol gyi gzugs stong pa nyid dang /_mtshan ma med pa dang /_smon pa med pa'i rnam par mthong ba zhes bya ba rnam par thar pa dang po dang /_phyi rol gyi gzugs med pa'i 'du shes kyis nang gi gzugs de bzhin du mthong ba zhes bya ba ni gnyis pa dang /_nang dang phyi rol gyi
[\[17a.5\]]gzugs med pa'i 'du shes kyis gzugs rnams mngon sum du nye bar rdzogs par byas te/_gnas pa zhes bya ba gsum pa dang /_nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi pa dang /_rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa lnga pa dang /_ci yang
[\[17a.6\]]med pa'i skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa drug pa dang /_'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la snyoms par 'jug pa bdun pa dang /_'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa ni brgyad pa ste/_'di dag rnams dag pa ni/_sna tshogs rdo rje'i zur bzhi dang logs bzhi'o/_/rdo rje theg pa'i
[\[17a.7\]]chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni sna tshogs rdo rje'i lte ba'i steng gi rim pa dang /_'brel pa'i rdo rje'i thig dang yang dag par ldan pa'o/_/'bras bu dbye bas 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i ri'i rtse mo shin tu mtho ba'i bye brag gis sna tshogs rdo rje'i rtse mo nyi shu'o/_/rten dang brten pa'i dbye bas sa lnga ni ngos
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]rnams dang steng ngo /_/gos pa med pa'i chos gcig dang /_du ma ji ltar rigs pa rab tu ston pa ni/_lha'i gnas kyi sna tshogs pad+ma'o/_/byang chub kyi sems yongs su smin par byed pas nyi ma'i gdan dang ldan pa'o/_/byang chub kyi sems kyi myu gu 'phel bar byed pas zla ba'i gdan dang ldan pa'o/_/_
[\[17b.2\]]snying rje'i bdud rtsis yongs su gang bas na bum pa brgyad do/_/chos kyi 'od kyi sgron ma'i grags pa ni dri zhim pa'o/_/chos kyi zas ni bshos gtsang ste/_de lta bu ni dkyil 'khor gyi de kho na nyid do/_/lha'i de kho na nyid brjod par bya'o/_/de la rnam par shes pa'i phung po dang /_zhe sdang chen po shin tu rnam par
[\[17b.3\]]dag pa dang /_chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes ni bcom ldan 'das so/_/'gro ba thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa bsdus pas gnag pa ni nag po'o/_/brtags pa'i yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa nyid gshin rje mthar byed pa'i phyir gshin rje gshed do/_/shin tu gdug pa can drag po zhi bas
[\[17b.4\]]mi 'dul la khro bo chen po'o/_/rnam thar sgo gsum rnam par dag pa zhal gsum mo/_/pha rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs pas phyag drug go/_/ser sna la sogs pa 'jig par mdzad pas rdo rje la sogs pa drug phyag na bsnams pa'o/_/zhe sdang gi cha'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa 'jig pas
[\[17b.5\]]sbrul gyis brgyan pa'o/_/tshogs gnyis yongs su rdzogs pas rang dang mtshungs pa'i ye shes la 'khyud pa'o/_/rtag tu sems can gyi don mdzad pas lhan cig skyes pa'i bde ba'i ngo bo'o/_/chos kyi sku nyid kyi phyir longs spyod rdzogs pa dang /_sprul pa'i sku mdzad pa'o/_/gzugs kyi phung
[\[17b.6\]]po dang gti mug chen po rnam par dag pa dang /_me long lta bu'i ye shes ni bcom ldan 'das gti mug gshin rje gshed do/_/gzhan ni snga ma bzhin no/_/gti mug gi cha'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i phra ma chen po dang /_tshor ba'i phung po rnam par dag pa dang mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes ni
[\[17b.7\]]bcom ldan 'das phra ma gshin rje gshed do/_/lhag ma ni snga ma bzhin no/_/nga rgyal gyi cha'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang /_'dod chags chen po dang /_'du shes kyi phung po rnam par dag pa dang /_so sor rtog pa'i ye shes ni/_bcom ldan 'das 'dod chags gshin rje gshed do/_/'dod
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]chags kyi cha'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang /_phrag dog chen po dang /_'du byed kyi phung po rnam par dag pa dang /_bya ba nan tan gyi ye shes ni bcom ldan 'das phrag dog gshin rje gshed do/_/phrag dog gi cha'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang /_'jig tshogs la lta ba dang /_shes
[\[18a.2\]]bya'i sgrib pa dang /_phung po'i bdud la dad pa rnam par dag pa ni/_bcom ldan 'das tho ba gshin rje gshed do/_/mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi rjes su mthun pa'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang /_mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang /_'dod pa'i sgrib pa dang /_nyon mongs pa'i bdud la brtson 'grus rnam par
[\[18a.3\]]dag pa ni bcom ldan 'das dbyug pa gshin rje gshed do/_/mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi rjes su mthun par nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang /_las kyi sgrib pa dang /_lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa dang /_'chi bdag gi bdud la dran pa rnam par dag pa ni bcom ldan 'das pa pad+ma gshin rje gshed do/_/mi
[\[18a.4\]]mthun pa'i phyogs kyi rjes su mthun pa'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang /_skye ba'i sgrib pa dang /_tshul khrims dang /_brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa dang /_lha'i bu rnam par g.yeng byed bdud la ting nge 'dzin rnam par dag pa ni bcom ldan 'das ral gri gshin rje gshed do/_/sa'i khams
[\[18a.5\]]dang thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_byams pa chen po'i ngo bo nyid rdo rje tsartsi ka'o/_/chu'i khams dang smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_snying rje chen po'i ngo bo ni rdo rje phag mo'o/_/me'i khams dang stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_dga' ba chen po'i ngo bo ni rdo rje dbyangs can ma'o/_/rlung
[\[18a.6\]]gi khams dang /_ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_btang snyoms chen po'i ngo bo ni rdo rje gau rI ma'o/_/phyi rol gyi gzugs la sogs pa dag pa ni thod pa bzhi'o/_/nang dri zhim pos kyang bkang ba ni/_chos kyi dbyings kun du 'gro'o/_/pha rol tu phyin pa sa dang sbyar ba yang brtag par bya'o/_/_
[\[18a.7\]]stobs dang ma 'dres pa la sogs pa ma bris pa ni gzhung mangs kyis dogs pas 'jigs pas so/_/de lta bu ni lha'i de kho na nyid do/_/de nas slob dpon gyi las te bsrung ba'i dam tshig dang /_bza' ba'i dam tshig bsgrub pa rgyud de dang de dag bstan pa'o/_/bdag bsrung ba ni so so 'brang
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]ma'i dkyil 'khor dang sgrub thabs bstan pas so/_/slob dpon 'jug pa ni gtor ma byin te/_de la rnal 'byor bzhi dang ldan pa'i slob dpon gyis bca' ba dang /_myang ba dang /_btung ba bldag pa la sogs pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa dri dang /_phreng ba dang /_byug pa dang /_phye ma dang /_gos
[\[18b.2\]]dang /_gdugs dang /_rgyal mtshan dang /_dril bu la sogs pa'i sgra chen po kun rdzob tu rdzogs pa dang bcas pa'i gtor ma shing rta bkang ba'am/_ma 'byor na nas kyi khur ba'am/_'bras chan nyung shas tsam dang bcas pa'i chu khyor ba gsum tsam yang rung ngo /_/de nas khro bo zhags pa
[\[18b.3\]]dang lcags kyu la sogs pa thogs pa spros te/_phyogs skyong ba rnams snying ga nas lcags kyus bzung zhing /_mgrin pa zhags pas bcings nas drangs par bsam mo/_/de la oM hrIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tA na na hUM hUM phaT phaT/_sarba duSh+TAn sa pa ri wA ra mA kAR+Sha ya dzaHzhes bya bas dbang po

[\[34a.1\]]gnas bzhi ru/_/'byung chen bzhi yi dkyil 'khor ni/_/yi ge bzhi la dbyibs mdog ldan/_/ba dan la sogs mtshan byas pa/_/bsams te rlung la sogs bskyod pa/_/rdo ba dag kyang 'bab gyur na/_/sems ldan 'bab pa ci zhig smos/_/ye shes babs nas 'phar gyur na/_/_

[\[34b.1\]]na rdo rje'i lag na 'dug/_/khyod kyis rtag tu gzung bar bya/_/phyag na rdo rje brtul zhugs brtan/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta sid+d+hi badzra sa ma ya tiSh+Tha maM/_e Sha s+t+waM d+ha ra yA mi badzra satwa hi hi hi hi hUM/_thog ma tha ma med pa yi/_/rdo rje sems dpa' dga' ba che/_/kun du bzang po kun bdag nyid/_/rdo rje

[\[35a.1\]]bzhin du/_/grub pa'i rdo rje dril bu 'di/_/khyod kyis dad pas rab zung la/_/rdo rje khyod kyis slob ma bsdus/_/ming yang sngon dang 'dra bar sbyin/_/de nas bla mas tshig 'di brjod/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi ral gri che/_/khams gsum kun gyis phyag byas pa/_/las

[\[35b.1\]]dbul bar bya/_/bla mas bzhes te byin brlabs la/_/sbyor ba'i cho gas mnyes par bya/_/bde ba mthe bong srin lag gis/_/slob ma'i kha ru dbab par bya/_/bde ba'i btung ba rin chen de/_/brtan pa'i blo yis btung bar bya/_/a ho su kha zhes kyang smra/_/de nas bu mo mig yangs
[\[35b.2\]]mo/_/mdzes shing nu ma rgyas pa zhig_/rang gi bu la sbyin par bya/_/mgo bor lag bzhag gsang ba gtad/_/de yi gzungs ma legs sbyin mo/_/de dang bde ba myang bar bya/_/de nas slob dpon shes rab dang /_/bcas pas dkyil 'khor lha de nyid/_/slob dpon las rnams
[\[35b.3\]]bstan par bya/_/ji ltar dbang bskur la sogs 'dis/_/sangs rgyas sogs kun thob pa bzhin/_/byang chub spyod sogs gzhan dag dang /_/'dul sogs dge bas de bzhin min/_/de bas dam tshig bus srungs shig_/rtag tu sdom pa yang bsrung ngo /_/sha lnga bdud rtsi lnga bza' ste/_/_

[\[71b.1\]]'dzin/_/tshul khrims sdom dang dam tshigs nyams pa ji snyed bshags/_/bdag gis bgyis dang de bzhin bgyid du stsal/_/nyan thos rang rgyal theg pa chen po'i dge ba'i tshogs/_/slob dang mi slob sems kyis grogs su gang gyur pa/_/'das dang ma 'ongs da ltar dge la rjes yi

[\[73a.1\]]sems phab pas/_/sa stengs sa 'og sa bla yi/_/gnas su sku gsung thugs bsams te/_/ma yengs don grub bzlas par bya/_/oM kA la rU pa hUM/_'dis ni brgya byin la sogs pa brgyal bar byed pa'o/_/oM ya ma rA dza/_sa do me ya/_ya me do ru/_Na yo da ya/_ya da yo
